</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхитительный.html>восхити́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosxitítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>amazing, delightful, admirable <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">causing wonder and amazement</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***восхитить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восхитить.html>восхи́тить</a> (26026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въсхытити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭsxytiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fascinate, to snatch away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхитить.html>восхити́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosxitítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхищать.html>восхища́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enrapture, to delight, to ravish</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхитительный.html>восхити́тельный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vosxitítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхищение.html>восхище́ние</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vosxiščénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly an independent borrowing of the same Old Church Slavonic word as above. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-хи́тить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-xítitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> high-style</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lift up</li></ol>

<li>to be carried away</li>

***восхищающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восхищаться.html>восхища́ющийся</a> (6478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***восход.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восход.html>восхо́д</a> (9710)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восходить.html>восходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восход.html>восхо́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosxód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восход.html>восхо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восход.html>восхо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восход.html>восхо́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rise</li>
<li>sunrise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восход.html>восхо́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнца</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vosxód</b> sólnca</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sunrise</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> east</li></ol>

***восходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восходить.html>восходи́ть</a> (16305)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восходить.html>восходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взойти.html>взойти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ascend, to climb, to go up, to mount</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go back (to a particular time)</li></ol>

***восхождение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восхождение.html>восхожде́ние</a> (11069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхождение.html>восхожде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosxoždénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхождение.html>восхожде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхождение.html>восхожде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхождение.html>восхожде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ascent, rise <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of ascending; motion upwards</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***восьмеро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a> (30755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vósʹmero</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eight (in a group together), eight of them
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> časóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight watches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> očkóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight pairs of glasses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> iz nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight of us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas býlo <b>vósʹmero</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were eight of us</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The nominative of a collective numeral governs the genitive plural of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. The other cases agree with that of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. Not used with feminine nouns. Used mostly when speaking of children and with a few nouns that are used in the plural only, such as <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>, or with pronouns.
</p>

***вот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> (47)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ото.html>ото</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вото</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">oto</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vot</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>here (is), this (is)
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> moj dom.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Here/this is my house.</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li>there
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> tebé raz!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There you are!</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> i vsjó!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That’s all!</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> čelovék!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a man!</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>во́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vót</b> gde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">here’s where</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">вот-во́т</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vot-vót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">just about to; on the point of</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vot</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>here, look (at it)</li>
<li>take it! (when offering something, casual)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">here, look</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотри́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smotrí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляди́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gljadí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глянуть.html>гля́нь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gljanʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">take it</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">very casual</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуть.html>воткну́ть</a> (7684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">во-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ткнуть.html>ткнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуть.html>воткну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">votknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втыкать.html>втыка́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in, into)</i>, to drive <i>(in, into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воткнуть.html>воткну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>votknútʹ</b> kol v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive a stake into the ground</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вотчина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вотчина.html>во́тчина</a> (25670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вотчина.html>во́тчина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vótčina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вотчина.html>во́тчины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вотчина.html>во́тчины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вотчина.html>во́тчин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>patrimony (also figuratively), (patrimonial) estate</li></ol>

***воцариться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воцариться.html>воцари́ться</a> (10475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">во-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царить.html>цари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воцариться.html>воцари́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vocarítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">воцаря́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ascend the throne</li>
<li>to set in, to be established
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воцариться.html>воцари́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тишина.html>тишина́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vocarílasʹ</b> tišiná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">silence fell</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воцариться.html>воцари́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчание.html>молча́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vocarílosʹ</b> molčánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">silence reigned</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семья.html>семье́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:воцариться.html>воцари́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v semʹjé <b>vocarílsja</b> mir</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the family began to live in peace</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воюющий.html>вою́ющий</a> (1674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воюющий.html>вою́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vojújuščij</span>)

***впадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a> (6953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">впад-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(river)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to flow <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><i>(a condition)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to lapse <i>(into)</i>, to sink <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задумчивость.html>заду́мчивость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v zadúmčivostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́яние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v otčájanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give way to despair; be driven into despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v somnénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin to have doubts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> неми́лость</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v nemílostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into disfavour/disgrace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:детство.html>де́тство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v détstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enter one's second childhood; be in one's dotage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v protivoréčije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">contradict oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(cheeks, eyes etc.)</i> to sink in, to become hollow/sunken</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">впа(д)-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpa(d)-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
